  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_1f10d713-00fd-4e87-88f6-63c1f3f8dce1'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);

<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">She's fond of rock music that's why she's called rock chick. In fact, all these chicks are fond of rock music even though music doesn't have really im<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">She's fond of rock music that's why she's called rock chick. In fact, all these chicks are fond of rock music even though music doesn't have really important part in this series (except for book 6). If you haven't read this series, this book better be read in order.<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer416700700" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17844594197386236164"><b>I don't think I'd ever change my mind about Luke...</b><br/><br/>Nothing new, still love it. Do you think it's strange that Ava was upset that Luke dragged her off in a fireman's hold? I do. If someone wanted to cart me around as a show of possessiveness and need, well, let's just say I wouldn't be complaining. Mind you, I think it would probably hurt a little considering the muscles he's packing. Still, I'd suffer...lordy, how I'd suffer. <br/><br/>**********<br/><br/><b>To infinity and beyond stars...</b><br/><br/>It's still bloody brilliant. </span>
  <span id="freeText17844594197386236164" style="display:none"><b>I don't think I'd ever change my mind about Luke...</b><br /><br />Nothing new, still love it. Do you think it's strange that Ava was upset that Luke dragged her off in a fireman's hold? I do. If someone wanted to cart me around as a show of possessiveness and need, well, let's just say I wouldn't be complaining. Mind you, I think it would probably hurt a little considering the muscles he's packing. Still, I'd suffer...lordy, how I'd suffer. <br /><br />**********<br /><br /><b>To infinity and beyond stars...</b><br /><br />It's still bloody brilliant. I still love Lucas Stark. The Hot Bunch Rules. The Rock Chicks are awesome.<br /><br />Of course, I'm not changing my ratings. Of course, it's still my favourite in this series. Of course, I'll probably listen to it again very soon.<br /><br />Listening to <i>Rock Chick Revenge</i> is my happy place. I always finish with a smile on my face and plan to visit with David Gandy...I mean Lucas Stark again soon.<br /><br />Peace and Love, Peoples...peace and love... 😉❤<br /><br />***********************************<br /><br />More dribble and drool from my previous visits...<br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Finished my re-read/listen and it's still 5-star magic.<br /><br />I'm currently reading The Scot Beds His Wife by Kerrigan Byrne and my two book worlds collided. I would LOVE to "see" Luke Stark in a kilt. <br /><br />Soooo Kristen Ashley, do you think you could whip me up a little <b>Hot Bunch goes Highlander?</b> That would be great, please and thank you's.<br /><br />I'll give it a week or two, but I bet I will be visiting the Rock Chicks again soon.<br /><br />********<br /><br />Luke is AWESOME!!<br /><br />Luke is SEXALICIOUS!!<br /><br />Luke can lift Ava in a fireman hold.<br /><br />Luke won't dance...but he'll ROCK YOUR WORLD!!<br /><br />Sigh...Lucas Stark has a mustache...and he's not afraid to use it. ;-)<br /><br /><br />Ava's cool too...but Luke Stark...makes me go hmmmm. :-) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer597637695" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4929698293396387901"><b>5 ‘I need cookies’ stars!!!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/df45b033-81c3-4a74-9c41-ffb1aa153512_zps6e6dfa7c.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418705i/829324.jpg' alt=' photo df45b033-81c3-4a74-9c41-ffb1aa153512_zps6e6dfa7c.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>OMG I love me some LUKE STARK!!! Okay... now thats out of the way, on to the review! <br/><br/>Ava Barlow is a changed woman. After being a little overweight, wearing glasses, and having mousy brown hair most of her life, she has decided to make a change. Five years ago, she saw the man she has always had feelings for, Luke Stark, at a funeral. After some crude comments from her nasty sisters, she vowed she wouldn’t see him until she transformed herself. And thats exactly wh</span>
  <span id="freeText4929698293396387901" style="display:none"><b>5 ‘I need cookies’ stars!!!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/df45b033-81c3-4a74-9c41-ffb1aa153512_zps6e6dfa7c.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418705i/829324.jpg" alt=" photo df45b033-81c3-4a74-9c41-ffb1aa153512_zps6e6dfa7c.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>OMG I love me some LUKE STARK!!! Okay... now thats out of the way, on to the review! <br><br>Ava Barlow is a changed woman. After being a little overweight, wearing glasses, and having mousy brown hair most of her life, she has decided to make a change. Five years ago, she saw the man she has always had feelings for, Luke Stark, at a funeral. After some crude comments from her nasty sisters, she vowed she wouldn’t see him until she transformed herself. And thats exactly what she did. With her transformation came a lot of man trouble. A lot. She has terrible luck when it comes to men. So she’s sworn them off. No men for Ava, just her b.o.b. But now, her best friend Sissy is in trouble. Ava wants to help her, but she needs help. Help from Luke and the Hot Bunch. I just love Ava’s reaction when she meets all the Hot Bunch...<br><i>
  <blockquote>I figured the Nightingale Investigations job application form had the question "Are you hot? Yes. No. If you answered no, please exit the building.”</blockquote>
</i><br>Luke cannot believe his eyes. He doesn’t even recognize Ava at first... Ava. The girl he’s known since she was eight and he was twelve. Someone who has always been there for him (apart from the last five years) <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“I've liked you since you were eight years old. You made me laugh. You understood me. You looked out for me when no once else fuckin' bothered and you acted like you thought I could move mountains and I needed someone who thought that about me.” </blockquote>
  </i>
</b> But this isn’t exactly the same Ava he remembers, and not just looks wise. Ava’s past has made her a bit bitchy towards men, Luke included. Luke will help Ava, but he wants to do more than help her. He wants her, in his bed, as his woman. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/50ec3de2-e888-4e4a-aa40-f45431a30984_zps1403b358.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418705i/829325.jpg" alt=" photo 50ec3de2-e888-4e4a-aa40-f45431a30984_zps1403b358.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>
  <blockquote>“You’ve been mine since you were eight.” </blockquote>
</i><blockquote> It isn’t easy for Ava to trust a man. Not after she has been burned so many times. But she trusts Luke. She just doesn’t want to get hurt. She’s worried he has feelings for someone else and she knows if she gives him the final piece of herself, and he destroys it, there will be nothing left. <br><i><blockquote>“Luke, you have to know, it won’t be like the other guys. If it’s you, it’ll be worse.”<br>My voice went softer, lower, barely a whisper.<br><b>“If this goes bad, it’ll destroy me.” </b>
</blockquote></i>
</blockquote><br>When it’s all said and done, will Ava be able to give Luke herself, trust him? Or will she stay determined to keep her heart safe and be alone... <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/17c64646-7a44-458d-b32b-b4cd28cd13c1_zpsb86c242e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418705i/829326.jpg" alt=" photo 17c64646-7a44-458d-b32b-b4cd28cd13c1_zpsb86c242e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Let me just tell you right off the bat... there will be a lot of quotes and gushing from here on out. I love these books! LOVE THEM! This book, and Vance and Jules book are both my favorite so far, I can’t choose! I just love everything about them... <br><br><b>The HUMOR</b><br><i>
  <blockquote>
<u>How the HOT BUNCH works...</u><br>“He isn't my man."<br>"Girl, it don't matter you don't think he is, he thinks he is. Therefore in Badass Motherfucker Land, that means he is.” <br><br><u>Ava’s inner dialogue (good Ava.... bad Ava...) </u><br>“Oh my goodness, Luke’s massaging your arm! Isn’t that sweet? Good Ava trilled in my ear. <br>Jump him! Rip his pants off! Bad Ava shouted in my other ear.” <br><br><u>Overall, Ava was just pretty funny</u><br>“Fuck buddies don’t have rules. It’s like being in a fight club. The first rule of fuck buddies is… there are no rules.” I was making this up as I went along. I had no idea if fuck buddies had rules. I’d never had a fuck buddy. I’d never even wanted one. Hell, I didn’t want one now!” <br><br><u>And so was Luke...</u><br>“You leave me cuffed, I’ll never speak to you again,” I told him.<br>“Babe,” now he sounded amused, “that’s a good thing. You got a mouth on you.”<br><br><u>Then of course, theres Tex :D </u><br>“I ain’t cuffin’ Luke to no bed,” Tex boomed, tearing me away from my intriguing thoughts. “Fuck, I’m not cuffin’ Lee or Vance to a bed, either. Those boys would lose their badass motherfucker minds. I got a girlfriend and fifteen cats. I get tortured and killed, who’s gonna take care of Nancy and my kitties?” </blockquote>
</i> <b>The SEXY</b><br><i>
  <blockquote>“You’re gonna be in my bed and not like last night. I’m gonna give you a taste of me and I’m gonna take more than a taste of you.”<br><br>"I'm not lettin' you go. I'm not lettin' you push me away and I'm not giving up. I'm gonna keep working until I piece together what they stole from you. I'm gonna keep at you until you let me in. I'm not gonna stop until you tell me you're mine, until it comes straight from your mouth, preferably when I'm deep inside you and you're lookin' at me like you look at me when I'm close to makin' you come." </blockquote>
</i> <b>And the SWEET</b><br><i>
  <blockquote>
<u>Luke made me SWOON</u><br>“Get this into your head Ava, I'm not gonna do anything to fuck this up between us but I'm also not gonna let you do anything to fuck it up either.” <br><br>“Life’s too short, I’m through talkin’. This is happening, we both know it, we both feel it and you even admitted it. Ava Babe, stop fighting it.”</blockquote>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/6aaa636e-0e70-4cca-9abf-a4620b6e614a_zpsdca900fb.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418705i/829327.jpg" alt=" photo 6aaa636e-0e70-4cca-9abf-a4620b6e614a_zpsdca900fb.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Then there is the action... there is always some action in a Rock Chick book. This one has plenty. Between Sissy’s problem’s coming to bite Ava, to her crazy ass ex coming back in the picture, there is never a dull moment! We catch up will all our favorite Rock Chicks, and members of the Hot Bunch! Then we get to meet a man named Ren. I loved Ren! Can’t wait to read more about that guy ;)<br><br>I loved the history between Luke and Ava. Luke was sweet, sexy, protective, and I couldn’t wait for him to give those little smirks! He was patient with Ava. Ava worked my nerves at time, but all of her actions and the way she tried to guard her heart were done for a good reason. I understood her. I ended up liking her a lot. She was tough, and super funny.<br><br>The ending of this one was fantastic! There is a wedding, pregnancy, and engagement... but you will have to read to find out who does what. Once again, another five star Kristen Ashely book! This woman’s writing and story telling abilities are just amazing! I am so happy I still have three more Rock Chick books to go! If you haven’t read this series, give it a go!</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer360010181" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17266845184476499084">*squeeeee* I LOVED THIS BOOK!!! What a winner!!<br/><br/>This is tied with books 1&4 for fav in the series so far! It had me laughing out loud, squeeing (out loud), tearing up, grinning for pages on end and fanning myself from the hotness (seriously, KA sure knows how to write make up sex!). PURE WIN!!!<br/><br/><b> <i> "I'm not lettin' you go. I'm not lettin' you push me away and I'm not giving up. I'm gonna keep working until I piece together what [they] stole from you. I'm gonna keep at you until you let me in. I'm no</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText17266845184476499084" style="display:none">*squeeeee* I LOVED THIS BOOK!!! What a winner!!<br><br>This is tied with books 1&amp;4 for fav in the series so far! It had me laughing out loud, squeeing (out loud), tearing up, grinning for pages on end and fanning myself from the hotness (seriously, KA sure knows how to write make up sex!). PURE WIN!!!<br><br><b> <i> "I'm not lettin' you go. I'm not lettin' you push me away and I'm not giving up. I'm gonna keep working until I piece together what [they] stole from you. I'm gonna keep at you until you let me in. I'm not gonna stop until you tell me you're mine, until it comes straight from your mouth, preferably when I'm deep inside you and you're lookin' at me like you look at me when I'm close to makin' you come." </i> </b><br><br>I apologize for the long gushy review - I just really loved it and had to share :P<br><br>Ava has known Luke since they were kids. But he went off to become a professional Badass fairly early on, and so they never actually got together. Unfortunately, her experience in life has led her to believe that all men are pretty much scum. But when her best friend's lying cheating scumbag of a husband finally pulls one stunt too many, she decides to find Luke, now a professional investigator/Badass and enlist his help to get some dirt on said scumbag. He of course is more than happy to help but Ava is nervous and wary about dealing with him due to some of her personal insecurities. But it soon becomes very clear that that was only the tip of the problem iceberg and when things blow up, and he realized she isn't going to share, he hand cuffs them together and takes them home to figure things out and the <i> "Badass Motherfucker Courtship" </i> begins :D<br><br><i> "I'll put money down that she's livin' with him in 4 days."...<br>"3 days."...<br>"A week, she's got spirit."...<br>I shook my head, I needed to focus...and go, go, go. <br>I opened the door.<br>Before it closed behind me, I heard Luke say strangely, "Tonight."<br>Then everyone laughed." </i> <br><br>I'll say this first. I. LOVED. LUKE. Seriously. WOW! What a character &lt;3<br><br><i> "I've known you since you were eight... I've liked you since you were eight," he said. </i><br><br>I fell in love with him since we first saw him several books ago in the series but he really just shines in this book. God <b> I love a man who is not only insanely HOT, brutally honest, defends his woman to the ends of the earth and takes no shit from anyone about anything, but at the same time has a deeply soft side </b> that with which he deals with Ava. He just was seriously <i> functional </i>, and a totally swoony over-protective Alpha Badass (yes, with a capital B) who was really creative with his handcuffs and had no problem literally ripping the clothes off his girl *waggles eyebrows*.<br><br>I just loved how tolerant, understanding and patient he was with Ava. He really truly understood how how deep her hurt goes and how much it has made her wary and untrusting and he's just so willing to show her through determination and rock steady efforts that he's not like the other men who have hurt her before and that he's absolutely, 100% seriously into her.<br><br><b> <i> "Ava, you missed it when it happened so I'll clue you in. last night, around the time you fell asleep against me, you became mine." </i> </b><br><br>Lol, but it was hilarious to finally see Luke deal with a woman of his own. We have been waiting for so long and seeing him handle it was hot-as-hell, hilarious and heart-melting.<br><br><i> "Jesus Christ," he muttered to the ceiling. "All those times I sat in the office and laughed my ass off at stories of Lee, Eddie, Hank and Vance. They should have fuckin' medals." </i><br><br>And honestly, a man who calls his woman 'babe' just melts my heart &lt;3<br><br>And Ava! Gah she just about broke my heart with her cuteness at times while other times I just wanted to throttle her. But she was a totally awesome addition to the Rock Chick group - a strong, independent character with a big heart. In the beginning she does do some things that are a bit annoying but, given some of her life experiences, her general wariness and mistrust of men is understandable.<br><br><b> <i> "He isn't my man."<br>"Girl, it dont matter you don't think he is, he thinks he is. Therefore in Badass Motherfucker Land, that means he is." </i> </b><br><br>And what makes it okay is that Luke sees riiiight through her so her behaviour doesn't actually ever come between them.<br><br><i> "You wanna taste me?" he murmered.<br>Yes, I wanted to taste him. I would pay every penny of Aunt Ella's inheritance to taste him.<br>"No," I lied.<br>He did a full grin this time, a full satisfied grin. It was hot, so hot my knees totally buckles and he took all my weight into his body.<br>"Liar," he whispered, knowing he had me. </i><br><br>And he just keeps relentlessly working at their relationship, never giving up on her, and yet never giving in to her insecurities, until she feels safe enough to let her walls down and truly give her heart over to him.<br><br><b> <i> “Daisy said to me that I was trying to find ways to protect my heart but I was doing it wrong. She told me the best way to protect my heart was to trust it to someone who will protect it for me”.<br>More silence but his body went completely still.<br>“That’s you. It’s always been you.” </i> </b><br><br>Their chemistry was intense! You totally felt it! They had a bit of a rough start - lots of interruptions (buzzers, phone calls etc lol), but once they finally came together... *fans self*<br><br><i> "Oh my God, you totally need to fuck him or you're going to spontaneously combust." </i><br><br>And they worked through the bulk of their issues by about the 70% mark so we got to see them completely and acceptingly together as a couple for a good chunk of the book. Seeing them deal with some very painful and serious events that happen totally made my heart clench. It was heart-meltingly beautiful, at times very emotional and utterly squee-worthy.<br><br>KA is just absolutely BRILLIANT at writing families and conveying deep connections between characters. She is very subtle and direct in her writing style but you FEEL their emotions so strongly. It just feels so real. Her writing style is like no other. It hide nothing, implies nothing, its just in-your-face, straight up awesome story telling that sucks you right in.<br><br>This book was a bit emotionally deeper than the last few. It had my throat choked up and my eyes all misty more than a few times. Ava was reeeally hurt in her past and the tone come through in the story despite its overall typical 'Rock Chick' lightness. Something about it just really had my heart reaching out for both her and Luke.<br><br>The humour and the banter was just off the charts. Very few other writers have every made me laugh or squee as much as KA has. Everything from the vibrator burial scene to the betting pools over how it would take Luke to give Ava the business to Smithie getting treed by rabid rottweilers... so much fun! And of course, lets not forget the healthy dose of typical KA kidnappings, hostage situations, rescue missions, etc.<br><br>I love how, as the series progresses, we see more and more of the characters. What a HUGE core group - there must be at least like 25 of them and just the dynamic of all of them together makes for some absolutely BRILLIANT scenes.<br><br>Some pretty serious stuff goes down later in the book involving one of Ava's psycho ex's and when it does, seeing, literally e.v.e.r.y.o.n.e come together and mobilize to be there for her (and Luke) was so beyond heart warming. *mega shivers* it led to pages and pages of utterly squee-worthy scenes!! Including the first (INTENSE) Alpha showdown between two of the "good guys" and also what has to be THE most EPIC car chase scene in book history! I was grinning like an idiot when I was reading it.<br><br><b> <i> "Swear to God, these boys should be locked up. It isn't safe, men with that much testosterone coursing through their blood free to roam." </i> </b><br><br>I just love how all the Hot Bunch men in this series are the total macho Alpha badass do-not-mess-with-me men on the outside but are all heart-meltingly soft and sweet on the inside. SERIOUS SWOON MATERIAL!! ... have I used the word 'brilliant' yet? lol BRILLIANT BRILLIANT BRILLIANT!!!<br><br><b> <i> "I figured the Nightengale Investigations job application form had the question "Are you hot? Yes. No. If you answered no, please exit the building." </i> </b><br><br>oooo and there is a wedding at the end of this book - I won't spoil it with telling whose it is but it actually took me a little by surprise even though I've read all the books in order. So beautiful!<br><br>Can't wait for the next book! When this series is over, I'm gonna be seriously sad.<br><br>Here's how I see Luke and Ava:<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380382647i/740576._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="17266845184476499084" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer9511283936099041209"><br/><b>Re-read Review - August 28-29, 2013.</b><br/><br/>I've had trouble picking my "favorite" Hot Bunch hero, but after my re-read of the first 5 books, I can say, without a doubt, that Luke is the one. Of all the men so far, he's the most similar to the men of the Colorado Mountain series, and I adore them! Luke is super bad-ass Alpha - yes, with a capital A - and he's the most crude and outspoken and intensely sexual of them all. And that right there, my friends, is why I'm in love with him, and why he's numero </span>
  <span id="freeText9511283936099041209" style="display:none"><br /><b>Re-read Review - August 28-29, 2013.</b><br /><br />I've had trouble picking my "favorite" Hot Bunch hero, but after my re-read of the first 5 books, I can say, without a doubt, that Luke is the one. Of all the men so far, he's the most similar to the men of the Colorado Mountain series, and I adore them! Luke is super bad-ass Alpha - yes, with a capital A - and he's the most crude and outspoken and intensely sexual of them all. And that right there, my friends, is why I'm in love with him, and why he's numero uno, comprende?<br /><br />I fell hard for Ava, again. Such a sweetie. I just adore her, and she and Luke together are perfect!<br /><br />Such a great story, start to finish!<br /><br />Now on to Rock Chick Reckoning, Mace and Stella's story!<br /><br /><b>Original Review:</b><br /><br />Those of you who read my reviews know that I normally go on for paragraphs, close to chapters… except when it comes to Kristen Ashley books. The reason for that is twofold… <br /><br />1.	There are just soooo many things to love about her awesome books that I can’t seem to do them justice, even if I ramble on for pages.<br /><br />2.	There are already a bjillion reviews out there, all singing her praises, so I’m doing you a favor by not making you sit through one of mine... not for too long, anyway.<br /><br />That’s why I keep ‘em short. So here goes…<br /><br />Ava: ADORE her! <br /><br />Luke: Abso-fecking-lutely in love with him!<br /><br />The Story: All kinds of awesome. <br /><br />Lot's of extra time with other Rock Chicks and Hot Bunch guys. LOVE THAT!!<br /><br />Secondary Characters: They don’t feel secondary, ever. I love each and every one of them and unlike some books, they never, ever, EVER feel like filler.<br /><br />So that’s why I love this book, and why you, if you haven’t already, need to climb on the Kristen Ashley train!<br /><br />Woot! Woot! ROCK ON!<br /><br />4.5 stars<br /><br />-----<br />If you're a Kristen Ashley addict, or just interested in checking her books, be sure to stop by our <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/66492-kristen-ashley-addict-s-support-group" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley Addict's Support Group</a> here on Goodreads! <br /></span>

<div id="review_1509103900" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1509103900" />
    <a title="Jilly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25894509-jilly"><img alt="Jilly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1435955932p2/25894509.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1509103900?book_show_action=true">Jan 14, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jilly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jilly" href="/user/show/25894509-jilly">Jilly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=contemporary-fiction">contemporary-fiction</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1509103900" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7293150457759229799">My favorite Rock Chick book since the first one. Why? I have loved Luke for many books now, for one reason. Secondly, I love the Rock Chick world and crazy characters. How can I not love a book that has this quote:<br/><b>
  <i>Tex shouted, "Jee-zus, huggin' and cryin' and badass motherfucker showdowns in livin' rooms and takin' a break from the action to have Sunday breakfast with your man's mother, what the fuck? We gonna take a side trip to the mall next or do we want to find this fuckin' guy?"<br/><br/>"Actually</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText7293150457759229799" style="display:none">My favorite Rock Chick book since the first one. Why? I have loved Luke for many books now, for one reason. Secondly, I love the Rock Chick world and crazy characters. How can I not love a book that has this quote:<br><b>
  <i>Tex shouted, "Jee-zus, huggin' and cryin' and badass motherfucker showdowns in livin' rooms and takin' a break from the action to have Sunday breakfast with your man's mother, what the fuck? We gonna take a side trip to the mall next or do we want to find this fuckin' guy?"<br><br>"Actually, I could use a side trip to the mall," Sissy put in...<br><br>"I could go to the mall too," Daisy added....<br><br>"We goin' to find Jeremiah?" Olivia asked, following us....<br><br>"Yeah, after the mall," I told her.</i>
</b><br><br>See, a group of girlfriends taking time out of their catch-the-bad-guy schedule to go to the mall? I can totally appreciate that. Priorities, you know.<br><br>So, in this book ,we have Luke, the hottie from the last few books, getting together with Ava, a girl who lived across the street from him from the time she was 8 years old. Ava was a fat kid with glasses and grew up staying fat and feeling like crap about herself. She also had a crush on Luke since childhood and decided, after seeing him as an adult, that she was going to get her crap together, lose weight, and finally take a shot at him. Of course, life came along and she ended up with another guy who totally ruined her faith in men. She's sworn them off. But, after getting into a jam, she tries to hire Luke to help her. Of course, Mr. Alpha decides that she is his. "Me man. You woman. Me want. Unga Bunga!" Okay, so maybe that's not exactly what he says, but it is what he means.<br><br>Of course, the Rock Chicks and the Hot Bunch (the guys) have seen this scenario play out many times and they know exactly how things are going to go down.<br><br><b>
  <i>"So, we had a pool. Everyone threw down money on when they thought Luke would nail you. Mace won five hundred dollars...So, did he nail you or did you just sleep?"<br><br>"We just slept."<br><br>"New pool!" Shirleen shouted.</i>
</b><br><br>And, Shirleen gets to be Ava's Rock Chick mentor because it's her turn. It is epic! Shirleen is absolutely awesome.<br><br><b>
  <i>We arrived and Shirleen was on the phone, handset in the crook of her neck, peering into a hand-held mirror, plucking her eyebrows.<br>She dropped the mirror and tweezers upon seeing us. "Dorothea, gotta go, my girl's here with her girl. We gotta lock old Sissy down so the Italians don't get her. Long story, I'll tell you later..."</i>
</b><br><br>Another later epic moment is when the famous girl who Indy tazed in her book, and Daisy fought and Jet tazed in the last book, shows up. And, there is the best car chase scene ever with more cars involved than the Indy 500.<br><br>The only downsides to this book. There were two: First, there are so many people quoting Luke saying "I never expected to want you in my bed, but I always knew I wanted you in my life" like it is the sweetest, most romantic thing ever. I didn't feel that way at all. He says this after telling her that he always thought she was pretty, even when she was overweight, and that he always liked her personality. And yet, he then says he never expected to want her as anything more than a friend? Why? Because she was overweight and not attractive enough for him. He said that she was pretty, funny, and kind... .but it wasn't enough while she was overweight. He never wanted her in a sexual way until the only thing that changed about her was her weight. That's kind of shitty, really. How's he going to deal with her pregnant, or what if she can't lose her pregnancy weight right away? The best husbands are the kind that remind a girl that she needs to lose a few pounds, right girls?<br><br>The other problem I had with it showed itself to me after reading something written by my friend, Karly <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/story/show/412697-a-pissed-off-vampire-ninja?chapter=1">https://www.goodreads.com/story/show/...</a><br>It made me notice how Luke reacted when Ava had been inappropriately touched by her ex. It suddenly became all about him. She was even afraid to tell him what happened because she was worried about his reaction. Then, she had to try and calm him down and reassure him as if HE were the victim. It was weird. I get that any man would be angry in this situation, but he reacted like it was a personal affront that some other man dared to touch his property. Um.... no..... just no. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452944337i/17762911._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Center of the universe? You mean my Throne Room?..</i><br><br>......................<br>E.T.A...... Oh yeah, wtf is with Ava answering her phone "yo" every time? What, is she is twelve year old boy trying to sound cool? What grown-up woman answers her phone like that every.single.time? I mean, when she was happy, sad, angry, in the car with a kidnapper, at the hospital...<br>So freaking stupid!!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="7293150457759229799" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_261393466" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/261393466" />
    <a title="Baba  " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4669232-baba"><img alt="Baba  " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1564910043p2/4669232.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/261393466?book_show_action=true">Jan 13, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Baba  " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Baba  " href="/user/show/4669232-baba">Baba  </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer261393466" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18109073092814822231">Luke said to Ava:<br/><b>"There are two kinds of women. The ones you go to bed with and the ones you wanna wake up with. Lots of the first, not many of the last. If a man's lucky, he'll find the last."</b><br/><br/><b>Wow, loved it!</b> This was my very first taste of the Rock Chicks series and a friends-to-lovers story. My GR friends know that I'm not a reader who feels the urge to read a series in order. And Rock Chick Revenge can be read as a stand-alone. Unfortunately, Kristen Ashley's Play it Safe didn't work for me an</span>
  <span id="freeText18109073092814822231" style="display:none">Luke said to Ava:<br /><b>"There are two kinds of women. The ones you go to bed with and the ones you wanna wake up with. Lots of the first, not many of the last. If a man's lucky, he'll find the last."</b><br /><br /><b>Wow, loved it!</b> This was my very first taste of the Rock Chicks series and a friends-to-lovers story. My GR friends know that I'm not a reader who feels the urge to read a series in order. And Rock Chick Revenge can be read as a stand-alone. Unfortunately, Kristen Ashley's Play it Safe didn't work for me and I am really happy that I'm back in reader's heaven. Again. Admittedly, some parts of this story were a bit far-fetched and it was a bit <i>OTT</i> at times as well but then again, who cares? Holy cow, Ava can throw sass! Yes, Ava babe, you can glare all you want but it is true! Ava's got attitude and then some! She knows how to use her mouth (uh, pun intended). She is funny, sweet, caring, and <b>bitchy</b> as all get out! Luke. YOWZA!!! Love this guy! Another badass, hot as sin, fabulous specimen of a man. He's very, <b>verrry</b> bossy and demanding, yet extremely gentle, tender, and protective. Luke is a nice guy who's trying to protect and keep Ava safe. He does it in an ultra pushy, unbelievably blunt, tough guy, macho man way. Aw, yes, I already mentioned Ava's mouth:<br /><br /><i>"You leave me cuffed, I'll never speak to you again," I told him.<br />"Babe," now he sounded amused, "that's a good thing. You got a mouth on you."</i><br /><br />What follows suit is the famous Ava Barlow Silent Treatment and I enjoyed it!<br /><br />If you're in a bad mood then you should read Rock Chick Revenge. Jeez, this was loads of fun, fun, <b>fun</b> and I had a good laugh! This story is filled with so much banter, lots and lots of witty dialogs, great characters, and quite a lot of action and drama. It felt like an action-filled (love) comedy. Honestly, don't take this story too seriously. Even when they had a "serious" situation I just knew we'd be back on track in no time flat. I loved to see how Luke and Ava locked horns and when the Barlow Bitch Blood started to flash through Ava's veins…woot! It was incredibly entertaining. A total blast! Furthermore, I was so mesmerized by the amazing Luke Lip Fog as well! And guess what? A Bad Boy pursuing a Rock Chick with competition on his ass means…trouble (trouble with a capital T).<br /><br />The sex/love scenes were steamy, sizzling hot, and well-written. Even in bed the banter was ever-present.<br /><br /><i>"Make you a deal. Tonight I'll bring the cuffs. Whoever manages to get the other cuffed to the bed gets to play."<br />That was hardly a good deal for me.<br />"You just pointed out the obvious, you're stronger than me."<br />"Babe, you're not using your imagination."<br />I have a good imagination, Bad Ava reminded me, her voice dripping with anticipation.<br />Me too, Good Ava surprised me, her voice sounding dreamy.<br />I smiled slowly.<br />Then I said, "Deal."<br />He touched his lips to mine, eyes open, and murmured, "Never thought life could be this sweet."</i><br /><br />Ava had to wait more than twenty years to finally declare…<i>"I love you, Luke."</i> I think it was so worth the wait!<br /><br />Rock Chick Revenge is another compelling and great story written by the <i>amazing</i> Kristen Ashley. Highly recommended if you're in need of a hilarious, sweet, action-packed, and fast-paced love story! Enjoy!</span>
  <a data-text-id="18109073092814822231" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer12945335985008493757">Meet my Luke! YUM!<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379800208i/665692._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Reread on 9/11/13<br/>I still feel exactly the same way I felt the first time I read this book, only I'm even more in love with Luke now!! Ava too, but let's be honest, none of us care about anything more than Luke here, lol!!! No Seriously!! I must say, this has been my favorite book of this series. I've read all of these once back in January except Ally's, and there just isn't a comparison to Lucas Stark. I love when alpha men are blunt, straight to the point, but sorta the lethal</span>
  <span id="freeText12945335985008493757" style="display:none">Meet my Luke! YUM!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379800208i/665692._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Reread on 9/11/13<br>I still feel exactly the same way I felt the first time I read this book, only I'm even more in love with Luke now!! Ava too, but let's be honest, none of us care about anything more than Luke here, lol!!! No Seriously!! I must say, this has been my favorite book of this series. I've read all of these once back in January except Ally's, and there just isn't a comparison to Lucas Stark. I love when alpha men are blunt, straight to the point, but sorta the lethal silent type as well. I have loved all of the Hot Bunch and Rock Chicks, but for me, Luke and Ava will always hold a special place in my heart. :) <br><br>Original Review written January 2013<br>Luke Stark has ruined me for all other book boyfriends. After meeting him a few times in the other previous books, I was really looking forward to him getting his own story, WOW, there is no comparison to him. BY FAR, my favorite book of this series so far. I am in LOVE with Luke Stark. Literally, I could go on and on. <br><br><b>"Ava Babe, I'm tellin' you, you're gonna admit you belong to me because <i>you belong to me."</i><br>"Luke, please, let me go home."<br>"No fuckin' way."</b><br><br>Luke and Ava are just perfect. The story begins with Ava coming to Luke to ask for help with her friends crazy soon to be ex-husband. Ava has some insecurity problems not to mention she has decided to hate men from now on. Luke and Ava had grown up across the street from each other as kids until Luke graduated and gone. The last time they had spoken was when his father had died and she promised a beer later, but later never came. NOT because of Luke, because of something Ava overheard. So now it's new Ava and new hotter Luke and as in all the Rock Chick books, a good dose of trouble.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404773i/787965.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><br>We get more of the Rock Chick crew, more of the newly named HOT BUNCH, (yum) plus a side dose this time of car chases, kidnappings, and a hostage situation. Not to mention Ava had a crazy ex who Luke went after that seriously backfired. And let me just say the way Luke and Ava handled that situation was perfection.<br><br>Of course we get all of the hilarity out of this installment just like the others. Smithie finds himself tree'd with two dogs standing guard. Tex still yells at the customers and plays favorites on who is next in line and the girls still like all of their shopping, gossiping, and bad ideas. It was just the most awesome book. So awesome, I don't really know how to move on to the next one.<br><br><b>"This is the way it is for us right now. I know you fixed this place up but I'm not givin' up the loft so we're gonna have to work somethin' out about where we live, eat, sleep, and fuck. We last, you're gonna have to give up the Range Rover, they're dangerous because they roll easy and I don't like you drivin' it. We go the distance, we're havin' a small wedding, I'm not fuckin' dancin' and I want three kids, all boys, but if we have a girl she's not datin' until she's twenty-five, especially if she looks like you, got me?-Luke</b> <br>ummm, yea, I would have jumped him.<br><br>This man was sex on a stick the entire book. Doesn't beat around the bush and says exactly what he wants and does it. OMG, the guy wanted payments and punishments and I was trying to get in between him and Ava and take her them for her, seriously!! I was beggin' for my chance at a "Luke Lip Fog".<br><br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/mean%20girls%20raise%20hand%20gifs/luvbledrollgeek/GIFs/tumblr_lfxbh4XnPI1qzb2ai.gif?o=1" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <span>[image error]</span>
</a><br><br>I will end this with I want more Luke and Ava!! I am starting a petition!! I need more Luke and Ava. Who's with me?!?!?!?!</span>

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2318827186" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3738916775413353720"><b> 4 stars! </b><br/><br/><b> <i> “He isn't my man."<br/>"Girl, it don't matter you don't think he is, he thinks he is. Therefore in Badass Motherfucker Land, that means he is.” </i> </b><br/><br/>This is a book that truly surprised me with how much I enjoyed it. 26% in or so I thought the hero was a bit rapey, but then it got so so good and I ended up loving Luke.<br/><br/>Rock Chick Revenge is about former "fatty" (as she put in her own words) Ava who goes to an old friend Luke with a problem her best friend is having. Right away Luke is more than</span>
  <span id="freeText3738916775413353720" style="display:none"><b> 4 stars! </b><br><br><b> <i> “He isn't my man."<br>"Girl, it don't matter you don't think he is, he thinks he is. Therefore in Badass Motherfucker Land, that means he is.” </i> </b><br><br>This is a book that truly surprised me with how much I enjoyed it. 26% in or so I thought the hero was a bit rapey, but then it got so so good and I ended up loving Luke.<br><br>Rock Chick Revenge is about former "fatty" (as she put in her own words) Ava who goes to an old friend Luke with a problem her best friend is having. Right away Luke is more than happy to reunite, in fact he all but abducts Ava into his life. <br><br><b> <i> “I'm not stupid, I know your heart's involved in this and I've never, not once in all the time you've known me, given you the idea that I won't handle it with care.” </i> </b><br><br>My weakness with romance is an insecure heroine and angst. This book had heaps of both so I thoroughly enjoyed it. I loved Ava and her journey, how she didn't just give in to Luke and believed everything right away. Their relationship took work and Luke was willing to put in the time.<br><br>I also thought this book was funny as hell and almost no one pissed me off which is a miracle cause with this series, normally someone is pissing me off. I got frustrated at some times with how Luke treated Ava, but later he more than made up for it and I ended up loving him. Even if he was a little bit rapey.<br><br>I think I'm off to binge what's left of KA's back list. I don't wanna run out but her books are hitting the spot!!!<br><br><b> <i> “Ava, you missed it when it happened so I’ll clue you in. Last night, around the time you fell asleep against me, you became mine.” </i> </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1494101706i/22685352._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Follow me on ♥ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/rachelreadsravenously" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> ♥ <a href="http://rachelsreadsravenously.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> ♥ <a href="http://instagram.com/rachelreadsravenously" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> ♥ <a href="https://twitter.com/rayliz89" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> ♥</span>

Ava only sees him again at his fathers funeral, where she overhears her sisters making terrible comments about her due to her weight, and she vows next time she sees Luke she will have lost the weight.<br><br>5 years pass, but by the time she meets Luke again, she has been burned by men, and has sworn off them for good. <br><br>I love how Luke just fell for Ava, never expecting her to mean anything romantic to him (not due to her weight, but more due to her age the last time he really spent any time with her) It would not bother him one bit, if she put back on some of the weight she had lost - as long as she was happy, as to him, she was his "beautiful Ava"<br><br><br>And this is my Luke! <div id="review_3575771421" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3575771421" />
    <a title="moonlight ☾" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/37448930-moonlight"><img alt="moonlight ☾" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1590665419p2/37448930.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3575771421?book_show_action=true">Oct 02, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="moonlight ☾" class="user" itemprop="url" name="moonlight ☾" href="/user/show/37448930-moonlight">moonlight ☾</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/37448930-moonlight?shelf=favorite-heroes">favorite-heroes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/37448930-moonlight?shelf=friends-to-lovers">friends-to-lovers</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3575771421" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer441513022164002227">✰ <b>4 stars</b> ✰<br/><br/>okay there was so much happening in this book and I honestly thought<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1539051134ra/26420023.gif' width='300' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>which isn’t a bad thing because I was entertained throughout the whole book, but I also needed to take a breather a couple times (unlike the previous two KA books I’ve read where I binged both) lmaoo.<br/><br/><b>
  <u>Luke (H):</u>
</b><br/>It’s unfair how KA knows how to write swoon worthy heroes I can’t help but fall for. As my third KA book, I can’t choose between Luke, Mitch and Tack as my favorite. 😭 with each hero I come across, there’s so</span>
  <span id="freeText441513022164002227" style="display:none">✰ <b>4 stars</b> ✰<br><br>okay there was so much happening in this book and I honestly thought<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1539051134ra/26420023.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>which isn’t a bad thing because I was entertained throughout the whole book, but I also needed to take a breather a couple times (unlike the previous two KA books I’ve read where I binged both) lmaoo.<br><br><b>
  <u>Luke (H):</u>
</b><br>It’s unfair how KA knows how to write swoon worthy heroes I can’t help but fall for. As my third KA book, I can’t choose between Luke, Mitch and Tack as my favorite. 😭 with each hero I come across, there’s something special about them that stands out to me. In Luke’s case, I absolutely loved how he sees beauty from within. During Ava and Luke’s childhood, while everyone would make fun of her because of her weight, he would defend her from the bullies and had always seen her as beautiful because she was being herself. 🥺<br><br><b>
  <u>Ava (h):</u>
</b><br>so let’s talk about the amount of shit Ava went through in this book that she didn’t deserve:<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[✧ Her mom and two sisters making fun of her weight all those years ago, which caused her insecurity.<br>✧ She gets kidnapped 3-4 times in this book?? This was mainly what i was referring to when i stated so much happened in this book cause wtf, that’s actually insane. 😭<br>✧ Dom (Ava’s best friend’s husband) making disgusting moves on her when she clearly keeps telling him no.<br>✧ Noah Dexter (an ex) touching her in that one scene while Luke was also in the house, somewhere upstairs.<br>✧ Past ex boyfriends who did her dirty andd her dad leaving her (which was the cause of her hatred towards men) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>she's been through a lot that I just wanted to hug her. :( but ngl, I was also quite annoyed with her a few times, such as the way she constantly lied, mainly to Luke, and I wanted to shake her and say just tell him the truth orrr every time Ren (I love the guy, but not for Ava lmao) appears, it sometimes felt like she had feelings for him? something I wasn’t a fan of, especially (78% in the book):<br><br><b>No, I wasn’t okay. All of a sudden, my mind was filled with having sex with Ren under a warm, balmy, tropical, starry night and they were happy thoughts.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1498659542ra/23149055.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I was confused because she was in an exclusive relationship with Luke at this point so idk, it just put me off with her character? hence, I’m 50/50 with her. I felt for her because of the things she had to endure, but I also didn’t understand the way her mind worked at times lol.<br><br>The one thing I was drawn to with this book tho (aside from Luke) was the found family between the Rock Chicks/Hot Bunch. They gave me that fun, entertaining family you would never be bored around with vibes and I actually thought <i>most</i> characters in this universe were interesting - especially my baby Rennn. &lt;3</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1488176495" />
    <a title="Robin (Bridge Four)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14105531-robin-bridge-four"><img alt="Robin (Bridge Four)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473392517p2/14105531.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1488176495?book_show_action=true">Dec 31, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Robin (Bridge Four)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Robin (Bridge Four)" href="/user/show/14105531-robin-bridge-four">Robin (Bridge Four)</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=adorable-alphas">adorable-alphas</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=cotton-candy">cotton-candy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=super-sidekicks">super-sidekicks</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1488176495" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13182942966573458964"><b>3.5 I need cookies Stars</b><br/><br/>Another KA buudy read with my girls at <a>Buddies Books & Baubles</a><br/><br/><b>Vacillation</b> that pretty much sums up my experience with this book. One minute I love Luke, the next I think he is a total over the top alpha jerk. One minute I love Ava and the next I’m shaking my head at her naiveté and methods of coping. But just as soon as either one of those thing happen I flip again any I’m totally on team Luke or Ava and I want them to get it figured out sooner rather than later. <br/><br/>But the </span>
  <span id="freeText13182942966573458964" style="display:none"><b>3.5 I need cookies Stars</b><br /><br />Another KA buudy read with my girls at <a>Buddies Books &amp; Baubles</a><br /><br /><b>Vacillation</b> that pretty much sums up my experience with this book. One minute I love Luke, the next I think he is a total over the top alpha jerk. One minute I love Ava and the next I’m shaking my head at her naiveté and methods of coping. But just as soon as either one of those thing happen I flip again any I’m totally on team Luke or Ava and I want them to get it figured out sooner rather than later. <br /><br />But the thing I never vacillate on is that Kristen Ashley is a natural story teller. Yes some things are really over the top especially in this series. A few of my favorites even if they are <s>really</s> slightly over the top are:<br /><br />✔ - A kidnapping, <i>actually I think there were 4 kidnappings in this</i><br /><blockquote>
  <i> That was when I was kidnapped. * * * * *<br />They weren’t good kidnappers. I knew this because I got away</i>
</blockquote><br />✔- The heroine does something silly that puts her in even more danger. At least she wasn’t TSTL or anything but there is always the one time they should have listened to the alpha male but did their own thing anyway.<br /><br />✔ - More than one <b>hubba hubba chunk of burning love hot guy</b> is interested in said heroine and it drives the other alpha male crazy. *snickers* (cuz Luke kinda deserves this after incidents in the precious two books) *shrugs* <br /><br />✔ - Heroine Freak out that is hilarious.<br /><blockquote>
  <i>“Thank God it’s you. Chips Ahoy or Nutter Butter?” I asked instead of saying hello. <br />Riley laughed in my ear. “Neither, where are you?” <br />“King Soopers, and I had a shit night. I need processed cookie-type food.” <br />“No shit night is worth processed cookie-type food,” Riley told me.</i>
</blockquote><br />✔ - Hilarious side characters that might hinder more than they help but in a totally funny way.<br /><blockquote>
  <i>“So we had a pool,” Shirleen carried on. “Everyone threw down money on when they thought Luke would nail you. Mace won five hundred dollars.” Ho-ly crap. “So,” she went on. “Did he nail you nail you or did you two just sleep?” <br />For some reason, I answered her unbelievably nosy question. “We just slept.” <br />“New pool!” she shouted.</i>
</blockquote><br />✔ - A Alpha male who will not give up no matter how many silly things you do to push him away. It is never good for the heroine when they start listing things.<br /><blockquote>
  <i>“The second part you gotta get, babe, is that I’m not lettin’ you go. I’m not lettin’ you push me away and I’m not giving up. I’m gonna keep working until I piece together what your Dad and those assholes tore from you. I’m gonna keep at you until you let me in. I’m not gonna stop until you tell me you’re mine, until it comes straight from your mouth,”</i>
</blockquote><br />Luke was more Alpha Male than any of the others we have had to date. He pushed the limits a little far sometimes and even I thought it was a little too much. When Lee handcuffed Indy to the bed it was kinda cute but when Luke did something similar it really didn’t work out the same way and I was so angry at him. Still overall he was a good character and I enjoyed being involved in their love story. It took a while but I loved that they knew each other in childhood and reconnected romantically as adults.<br /><br /><b>There are just a few things that really bothered me.</b><br /><br />Luke going just a little too macho man. Ava using the silent treatment as a punishment against Luke, it was so childish and even though he decided to think it was cute I was annoyed. I also get the Ava was a bit heavy most of her life so she wasn’t used to male attention but she had four different men interested in her at the same time and she seemed to naïve about the entire situation and did a few things that if Luke had done them I would have been livid. And last but not least, Luke was apparently seeing someone when Ava came back into his life. Apparently it wasn’t serious aka exclusive but he just dropped her like a hot potato without any remorse or anything. So apparently he was kinda a man whore and she was just his latest piece so no big deal. It was just a little too much. I get it he is a super macho man and needs to get laid all the time so of course he’d have a woman or two at all times just for that.<br /><br /><b>Overall</b> none of these things were deal breakers for me and I really enjoyed how Ava and Luke’s story played out. There were a few really emotional scenes that totally got to me and even reminded me why I loved Lee so much. Another good addition to the Rock Chick gang. <br /><br />P.S. I’m totally going to take a trip to Denver because I really want to find the Nightingale offices and or Fortnums.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13182942966573458964" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1799036397" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1926676140746578997"><b>
  <u>Re-read: 14.03.2017</u>
</b><br/>I have <i>no fucking clue</i> as to why I suddenly started re-reading this book. Sure <b>Ava Barlow</b> (29) and <b>Lucas Stark</b> (33) are a cute couple, but this book is so far from my favorite, specially in this series... But Luke is hot. Very much so. <b>Lee</b> and <b>Ren</b>, too. Love them. The <b>Rock Chicks</b> though... I <i>so</i> do not get along with them. So why do I find myself coming fucking back all the fucking time :O!? I do understand that the <b>Hot Bunch</b> is worth is, but the girls? No so sure...<br/><blockquote>
  <b>
   </b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText1926676140746578997" style="display:none"><b>
  <u>Re-read: 14.03.2017</u>
</b><br>I have <i>no fucking clue</i> as to why I suddenly started re-reading this book. Sure <b>Ava Barlow</b> (29) and <b>Lucas Stark</b> (33) are a cute couple, but this book is so far from my favorite, specially in this series... But Luke is hot. Very much so. <b>Lee</b> and <b>Ren</b>, too. Love them. The <b>Rock Chicks</b> though... I <i>so</i> do not get along with them. So why do I find myself coming fucking back all the fucking time :O!? I do understand that the <b>Hot Bunch</b> is worth is, but the girls? No so sure...<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>His hand came up and his fingers wrapped around my head and the third hot guy in a day (or a little more than one, I didn’t know what time it was, I just knew it was dark outside) leaned forward and put his forehead against mine.<br>Lee’s forehead lean was a lot different than Luke’s or Ren’s.<br>Lee’s was scary.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445268775i/16623124.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b><u>First read review</u>:</b><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I figured the Nightingale Investigations job application form had the question "Are you hot? Yes. No. If you answered no, please exit the building.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b>So damn mixed up!</b> Here's the thing: I love <i>Kristen Ashley</i>'s males. Her writing for them is perfect. Great. Hot. Sexy. Perfect. BUT, (yes, there is a damn but here, too) I have problems with her damn female characters. They <b>annoy me to the point of wanting to slam my head into the wall</b>. Sometimes I get them, but most of <i>Kristen</i>'s females are in the late twenties and acts like they are sixteen. I have a huge problem with grown ups not acting their age, or not acting close to their age. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> “There are two kinds of women. The ones you go to bed with and the ones you wanna wake up with. Lots of the first, not many of the last. If a man's lucky, he'll find the last.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>It gets too much at times, for me it seems, since everyone else seem to <i>love</i> this series. I like it just fine, <b>the males really makes it worth it</b>, but I don't love it. This is my third book in <i>Rock Chick</i> series (yes, I jumped numbers: going from book one, to book six, to book five...) and it comes second on my list for this series so you understand that I didn't hate it. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I'm not stupid, I know your heart's involved in this and I've never, not once in all the time you've known me, given you the idea that I won't handle it with care.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Now that I've got that out of the way let's get to other things. <b>The story? Predictable</b>. A lot happened, but at the same time the book felt slow and it didn't <i>feel</i> like things happened. As you can tell: I have really mixed feeling about the book. I should, really, just give up this series...<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> “He isn't my man."<br>"Girl, it don't matter you don't think he is, he thinks he is. Therefore in Badass Motherfucker Land, that means he is.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1489534105i/22224211.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b><u>Quick basic facts</u>:</b><br><b>Genre</b>: - (Adult) Contemporary Romance<br><b>Series</b>: - Series, Book Five<br><b>Love triangle?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No, but there is another love interest. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Cheating?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>HEA?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Favorite character?</b> - Ren Zano<br><b>Would I read more by this author/or of series?</b> - Not of the series, I think. I've given up.<br><b>Would I recommend this book/series?</b> - Everyone else seem to love it, yeah?<br><b>Will I read this again in the future?</b> - No.<br><b>Rating</b> - 2.5/3 stars.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1462420742?book_show_action=true">Dec 07, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

<span id="freeTextContainer12964373342554385930"><b>5 Cookie Stars!!</b><br/><br/>Ava didn’t always look like she has now. She was a little chubby, wore glasses and had two bitchy older sisters that made her believe that she was ugly and nobody would ever want her. <br/>So, even having a crush for Luke since she was 8 years old, she didn't think we would ever look at her, so she promised herself that she would never see him again until she was in her perfect form. <br/>But in the meanwhile she had bad luck with guys and she also promised that she would never tangle hers</span>
  <span id="freeText12964373342554385930" style="display:none"><b>5 Cookie Stars!!</b><br><br>Ava didn’t always look like she has now. She was a little chubby, wore glasses and had two bitchy older sisters that made her believe that she was ugly and nobody would ever want her. <br>So, even having a crush for Luke since she was 8 years old, she didn't think we would ever look at her, so she promised herself that she would never see him again until she was in her perfect form. <br>But in the meanwhile she had bad luck with guys and she also promised that she would never tangle herself with a man again. <br>That is, until she see Luke again.<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380436157ra/881473.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Luke didn’t saw Ava for 5 years. She was one of the most important persons in his life but they somehow drifted apart after she reject all his phone-calls after his father’s funeral (well, she had her reasons! Read it!).<br>So when he finds her looking for him at his work, looking hot as hell and not even a bit resembling as the old Ava he knew, he knows he have to get her back. And preferentially try to get the old her in the progress. <br>And since she got herself in trouble (or weren’t the girls in this series ALWAYS in trouble) he have a lot of time do to that.<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419296i/831035.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For some reason this was the story I was most anxious to read. And with good reason, it was definitely my favorite book in the series (so far). It was more emotional, more personal, more angsty and it was more intimate than the others. <br>Although Lee is still my favorite (I think!!), Luke gives him a good fight. He was so great ;)<br>And Ava, even with her insecurities (that I kind of understood) I really liked her too. <br>The rest… the Rock Chicks and the Hot Bunch, were awesome as ever! ;)<br><br>For the millionth time I tell you: If you haven’t start reading this yet, you are missing a hell of a series! : ) </span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1942431801" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer5885845996157106404"><b>reread:</b> <br/>05/05/17<br/>7/11/17<br/>17/05/18<br/><br/><br/><blockquote><i>"And remember that time you sold a bag of oregano to Mitch and Josh Burk, telling them it was pot?"<br/><br/>"We needed money. There was a kiss tribute show coming up. They never figured it out, said it was the best weed they'd ever had."</i> </blockquote><br/><br/><b>3/5 stars</b> <br/><br/><b>edit 21/03/17: I originally rated this book 3.5 stars but after reading four of the other books in this series I've had to bring this rating down. The main characters in this story did not live up to the standard I think this seri</b></span>
  <span id="freeText5885845996157106404" style="display:none"><b>reread:</b> <br />05/05/17<br />7/11/17<br />17/05/18<br /><br /><br /><blockquote><i>"And remember that time you sold a bag of oregano to Mitch and Josh Burk, telling them it was pot?"<br /><br />"We needed money. There was a kiss tribute show coming up. They never figured it out, said it was the best weed they'd ever had."</i> </blockquote><br /><br /><b>3/5 stars</b> <br /><br /><b>edit 21/03/17: I originally rated this book 3.5 stars but after reading four of the other books in this series I've had to bring this rating down. The main characters in this story did not live up to the standard I think this series has. Ava was frustrating and often petty, thinking only of herself.</b><br /><br />I did enjoy this story although I'm getting a little frustrated with the main female leads in this series, they're all over the place and can't seem to set their minds on just one man. It was frustrating to see Ava continually string men along under the guise that she didn't know what she wanted and 'wasn't used to the attention'. Seriously, nobody can be that obtuse, even <i>if</i> they've never had much attention before. <br /><br />If this only happened in one of the stories in this series, it wouldn't bother me but it's become a running theme. And one I do not enjoy. It takes love triangles to a whole new level when she's bouncing between four different guys, all the while pretending not to notice she sending off mixed signals.<br /><br />I adore Luke, he's on of my favourites in the series (let's be honest, every one of the Hot Bunch are my favs lol) and the reason I still reread this book is for their history. I love that they had a childhood history where Luke was just as kickass as now, and stood up for Ava even when she wasn't a knockout gorgeous Rock Chick. When she was just little "fatty fatty four-eyes Ava", they still has something special. <br /><br />The usual drama (see: kidnapping[s], shootings, mafia members and the works) became a little monotonous throughout this book, but I always go back for the SWEET Luke and Ava parts and Ava and Lee's friendship. It's my favourite thing that the hot guys all have a special relationship with one of the other Rock Chick girls—nothing romantic, just a close bond because of everything they go through.</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer270118917" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer4831278279560212595">4 stars – Chick lit/Contemporary Romance/Romantic Suspense<br/><br/>If I rated this based on the heroine it would get 1 star because Ava topped the annoying b*tchometer until around the 65% mark and even after that was still ungrateful and somewhat irritating. Without a doubt, yummalicious, handcuff wielding, uber alpha badass Luke Stark made and saved this book. <br/><br/><a href='http://s1206.photobucket.com/albums/bb447/shawnarazz/?action=view&current=Handcuffs-1.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/>‘Nough said.<br/><br/>Peace Out and Rock On!<br/><br/>*****Edited from original rating/review*****<br/><br/>I bumped this from a somewhat lackluster 4 stars to a stronger</span>
  <span id="freeText4831278279560212595" style="display:none">4 stars – Chick lit/Contemporary Romance/Romantic Suspense<br><br>If I rated this based on the heroine it would get 1 star because Ava topped the annoying b*tchometer until around the 65% mark and even after that was still ungrateful and somewhat irritating. Without a doubt, yummalicious, handcuff wielding, uber alpha badass Luke Stark made and saved this book. <br><br><a href="http://s1206.photobucket.com/albums/bb447/shawnarazz/?action=view&amp;current=Handcuffs-1.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
