<div id="review_1057747095" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1057747095" />
    <a title="Choko" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27962805-choko"><img alt="Choko" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1475642755p2/27962805.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1057747095?book_show_action=true">Sep 17, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Choko" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Choko" href="/user/show/27962805-choko">Choko</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27962805-choko?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1057747095" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12262972272496501135"><b> *** 4 ***<br/><br/>A buddy read with the KA addicts from BB&B</b><br/><br/>I love this series. Is it perfect - faaaaar from it, if you judge it by the typical literary parameters. It is flawed, the characters are flawed, the interactions between them are flawed, everything is flawed!!! There are so many things wrong with the way the bossy alpha males treat their insecure but still strong and fighting rock-and-roll loving women, that sometimes I ask myself <b> what the heck am I reading and why do I keep on doing it... </b> T</span>
  <span id="freeText12262972272496501135" style="display:none"><b> *** 4 ***<br /><br />A buddy read with the KA addicts from BB&amp;B</b><br /><br />I love this series. Is it perfect - faaaaar from it, if you judge it by the typical literary parameters. It is flawed, the characters are flawed, the interactions between them are flawed, everything is flawed!!! There are so many things wrong with the way the bossy alpha males treat their insecure but still strong and fighting rock-and-roll loving women, that sometimes I ask myself <b> what the heck am I reading and why do I keep on doing it... </b> They are formulaic, over the top, crazy and very unlikely contemporary romances, brimming over the edge with sassy banter and macho grunts, a lot of shootings and many abductions.. . There is coffee drinking, pole dancing, gun toting, hot rod driving, a ton of shopping, and most of all, crazy mating rituals for alpha males and their challenging and wild females, who sometimes overdo the internal monologue.<br /><br /> I know it sounds cacophonous, maybe a bit tedious, even somewhat unreadable... And maybe, some of you would absolutely hate these series, possibly even the author and her writing. As I have said before, <b> it is not literature, people!!! </b> However, if you have already tasted some of KA's fair, and if what she serves up pleases your pallet, well then, this is the series for you!!! Because what she has in spades is <b> the incredible ability to craft a narrative in the most entertaining way possible with a simple language and a G-d given talent for storytelling!!! </b> And those of us who like to sit on her table and sample of her offerings as much as we can, we seem to turn a bit unreasonable when it comes to objectivity about her works. We keep coming back for more, and more, and more.... <br /><br />This book finally fond a worthy love interest for the hot and mysterious Luke S. from Nightingale Investigations, a.k.a. Hot Bunch Boys, in the person of Ava, a girls who has known him since she was 8 and he 12, and has been crushing on him ever since. She has all the attributes a new Rock Chick needs to fit in - brains, attitude, a challenging personality, the propensity to get in mortal danger and be a magnet for trouble. Things happen which give the perfect opportunity for Luke to protect and claim her, and as part as how these things go, she battles him kinking and screaming to the bitter end... From the first moment they lay eyes on each-other all of us know what will be the end result, but it sure is a fun ride getting to the inevitable end. <br /><br />As always, the ensemble of secondary characters is what makes this book. We know them, we love them and we keep on falling deeper and deeper for them. I do not even want to imagine a Rock Chick book without Tex, Duke or Daisy!!! <b> *shudders* </b> We need our doze of crazy! <br /><br />I am once again grateful for my buddy reading addicts and am looking forward to our next read together!!! Thank you and may all have many books and fun times reading! <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="12262972272496501135" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText11419313325293756305" style="display:none">One life altering moment has Ava vowing that the next time she sets eyes on childhood friend Luke, he will see a different movement. See Ava although always beautiful,struggled with her weight and after overhearing some vicious comments about her and Luke she vowed that never again would it be embarrassing to be seen together. Now Luke, never cared how Ava looked, he thought she was beautiful inside and out. <br /><br />Eight years later Ava has sought out Luke, who she heard was a private investigator needing his help at getting revenge when it comes to her best friends soon to be ex-husband, the cheating rat. It only takes one minute though as she walks through the door of the Nightingale offices to realize she is not ready to see Luke and tries a quick retreat, however Luke wants answers from Ava not to mention her in his bed. <br /><br />Things are only heating up as Ava finds herself being sought after by four different men, including Luke. Not to mention she has been kidnapped and seems to be the center of havoc in all different directions. With the help of the Rock Chicks, Ava is thrown from one situation to the next but the only thing she continuously is running from is her feelings for Luke, but he plans to extract them from her in all sorts of creative manners.<br /><br />I am torn between if Lee or Luke is my favorite, Luke is heart melting and swoon worthy. I loved this story it is a 50/50 on which one is my favorite.<br /><br />**Reread I would say this is a 50/50 on which is my favorite. Luke is a man you go gaga over, intense, straight speaking, and head over heels for Ava, she just doesn't know it.</span>

<div id="review_338659266" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

        <a title="Crystal~BIG book addict~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Crystal~BIG book addict~" href="/user/show/7270157-crystal-big-book-addict">Crystal~BIG book addict~</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer338659266" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer18097015582327872248">Even though I have read this book more than once, I just love it. Love Ava. Really love Luke. Love the Rock Chicks and the Hot Bunch. Can't get enough of them.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380379197i/735331.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Luke and Ava both deserve love and happiness. They were neighbors as kids and Ava always had a crush on Luke. After many years of being off on their own, they come together and Luke decides to quit messing around. Ava fights it (of course) but he's an alpha male so <b>no</b> really doesn't mean anything to him. <br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380379197i/735332.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380379197i/735333.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380379197i/735334._SX540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380379197i/735335.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380379197ra/735336.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>I just love these two together.</span>
  <span id="freeText18097015582327872248" style="display:none">Even though I have read this book more than once, I just love it. Love Ava. Really love Luke. Love the Rock Chicks and the Hot Bunch. Can't get enough of them.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380379197i/735331.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Luke and Ava both deserve love and happiness. <div id="review_261452565" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/261452565" />
    <a title="Nikki" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5279570-nikki"><img alt="Nikki" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1423057450p2/5279570.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/261452565?book_show_action=true">Jan 13, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nikki" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nikki" href="/user/show/5279570-nikki">Nikki</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5279570-nikki?shelf=kristen-ashley-why-so-awesome">kristen-ashley-why-so-awesome</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5279570-nikki?shelf=4-and-a-half-stars">4-and-a-half-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5279570-nikki?shelf=own-ebook">own-ebook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5279570-nikki?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5279570-nikki?shelf=delicious-hero">delicious-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5279570-nikki?shelf=hot-hot-hot">hot-hot-hot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5279570-nikki?shelf=favourites">favourites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5279570-nikki?shelf=hottt-hero">hottt-hero</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer261452565" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10583231594729644204"><b>
  <i>Recently re-read this and YIKES!</i>
</b> Totally loved it better the second go round - so much that I amped up my rating from a straight 4 stars to 4.5 with a lean more towards 5 (in GR standards).<br/><br/>Ava was much more easier to understand this go round. And I had TOTALLY forgotten about all of the amazing and awesome shit that happens in this story. Crazy exciting.<br/><br/>4.5 stars.<br/><br/>The Rock Chick series has proven itself as a bunch of cute and fun stories with hot alpha heroes and sassy heroines but I do feel </span>
  <span id="freeText10583231594729644204" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>Recently re-read this and YIKES!</i>
</b> Totally loved it better the second go round - so much that I amped up my rating from a straight 4 stars to 4.5 with a lean more towards 5 (in GR standards).<br /><br />Ava was much more easier to understand this go round. And I had TOTALLY forgotten about all of the amazing and awesome shit that happens in this story. Crazy exciting.<br /><br />4.5 stars.<br /><br />The Rock Chick series has proven itself as a bunch of cute and fun stories with hot alpha heroes and sassy heroines but I do feel they kind of follow a similar "formula". Lots of H/h chemistry and fireworks in the beginning; the h being crazy in love with the H and vice versa; then she pushes him away (sigh) because I don't know, he's too amazing?; cue misunderstanding or some other random silly behaviour (sigh); then it gets to about 65% when the h gives in and we finally get to see some awesome KA character/story development.<br /><br />I did love Luke and Ava in this and as long as I didn't let the RC formula affect me too much, <i>Revenge</i> was an exciting, fun romp of a story.<br /><br />Luke was a freaking overload of hotness. If ever I wished I could "watch" a KA book like a movie, now was the time. When Luke found out that Ava had turned up at the Nightingale offices and then stormed in with his hotness and his kickass mustache, I quivered! I could TOTALLY envision the sinfully hot Luke with stormy features, body coiled tight, darkening the entrance to the office and the air being thick with intense sexual energy. *swoon* Then he just became more amazing as the story went on.<br /><br />Ava touched me from the very beginning with the fact that she had been a chubby adolescent, turning into an overweight adult who decides to take control of her life and get fit and healthy (and amazingly smokin' hot along the way). As RC heroine standards go, Ava had occasional snark in the beginning but other than that she was a pretty kickass, sensible kinda gal.<br /><br />I loved Luke and Ava's history, I loved that Luke decreed that Ava had been <i>his</i> since they first met as kids. I even loved that in the story she had 4 guys panting after her at once, when she had never been the type of girl who'd received that kind of attention before. This affected me on a personal level because I was that girl too and have only just recently taken control of my life in the same way that Ava had.<br /><br />This was fabulous and had me by my heart and soul all the way through. I love Luke and Ava forever!!!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="10583231594729644204" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_280350714" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/280350714" />
    <a title="~ Becs ~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2626261-becs"><img alt="~ Becs ~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1388693144p2/2626261.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/280350714?book_show_action=true">Feb 19, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="~ Becs ~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="~ Becs ~" href="/user/show/2626261-becs">~ Becs ~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=alpha-hero">alpha-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=kindle">kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=romantic-suspense">romantic-suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=lost-love-rekindled">lost-love-rekindled</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=private-investigator-hero">private-investigator-hero</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer280350714" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12679946486746013866">Been waiting a while to get to Luke’s story and his Rock Chick as I have a little crush on him.<br/><br/>His Rock Chick is Ava. They grew up across the street from each other and she has been in love with him since she was 8. Ava grew up as an ugly duckling with 2 older and, at least in her mind, more beautiful sisters. Ava considers herself fat and wears thick glasses due to bad eyesight. Her sisters’ beauty only runs skin deep, however, as they cruel to Ava and makes her feel bad about herself the whole</span>
  <span id="freeText12679946486746013866" style="display:none">Been waiting a while to get to Luke’s story and his Rock Chick as I have a little crush on him.<br /><br />His Rock Chick is Ava. They grew up across the street from each other and she has been in love with him since she was 8. Ava grew up as an ugly duckling with 2 older and, at least in her mind, more beautiful sisters. Ava considers herself fat and wears thick glasses due to bad eyesight. Her sisters’ beauty only runs skin deep, however, as they cruel to Ava and makes her feel bad about herself the whole time she is growing up.<br /><br />Luke has always liked Ava and, when he went home for his father’s funeral, was happy to see her and said he would call and they would hook up. He did call but Ava ignored his calls due to the fact that she’d overheard her sister’s catty remarks about how fat she looked when she was hugging Luke at the burial. Ava decides this is a life-changing moment and decides to get in shape, lose weight and get contacts which she does successfully and now she’s a swan. She has a few disastrous relationships in the years that follow including one with a guy called Noah who stole her money and her jewellery left to her by her favourite aunt. She’s now sworn off men forever and vowed fidelity to a pair of vibrators.<br /><br />It’s now 8 years later and Ava decides to go to Luke in his capacity as a PI to investigate her best friend Sissy’s philandering husband who has been coming on strong to Ava and Sissy needs the dirt to divorce him. She walks into Nightingale Investigations and Luke doesn’t even recognise her she’s changed so much. He’s actually not happy with the change – she may be a knockout but he thinks she’s become hard and cold and a bit of a bitch over the years and vows to search for the Ava he once knew, believing that she’s in there, buried under the heartache. She chickens out of actually asking him for help and decides to go it alone. Her first foray into sneaky investigations ends in disaster with Luke catching her in Sissy’s house as it explodes in gunfire – a drive-by sending message to Dom<br /><br />Ava gets herself into a whole heap of trouble and Luke decides she is worth the effort and wants to protect her. We have the now familiar plot of the Rock Chick thinking herself not good enough for her guy and him coming on very strong and bashing his head against a wall trying to convince her they are good together. The rest of the Rock Chicks and the Hot Bunch all start laying bets on when the consummation will take place – and Ava and Luke have several hilarious moments of coitus interruptus before they finally get their act together.<br /><br />The real danger in the book to Ava comes out of nowhere and I was really shocked to see who it was and what he did – totally unexpected with what had gone before.<br /><br />There are some pretty hilarious moments in this one with Smithie getting trapped up a tree by a pair of rottweilers and Tod planning a vibrator burial ceremony to mention just a couple and it’s great to see all the regulars getting in on the action and a hint at Mace and Stella who are up next in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13065142.Rock_Chick_Reckoning__Rock_Chick__6_" title="Rock Chick Reckoning (Rock Chick #6) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Rock Chick Reckoning</a>.<br /><br />I did enjoy this but not quite as much the books that came before – maybe Ava was a little bit too annoying with her constant inner monologue with Good Ava and Bad Ava and she was a bit of a bitch to Luke sometimes who I adore. Then perhaps no one was going to be good enough for him as far as I was concerned. It ends with a wedding and happy news for one of the couples from the previous books.<br /><br />4 star romantic suspense.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12679946486746013866" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1002420819" class="readable"
              >

Her books make feel like I'm THE SHIT!!! I just feel so awesome after reading her books, like I could conquer the world, which is perfect right now because I'm 8 months pregnant, and I defi</span>
  <span id="freeText8265747701892214528" style="display:none"><b>5 THOUSAND MILLION STARS!!!!!</b><br><br>Me: This book is my favorite!<br>Hubs: I thought the last Rocker Chick book was your favorite.<br>Me: No! They just keep getting better, and I just love all of them! <br><br><b>My Luke:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407375931i/10683673._SX540_.jpg" alt="*-" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>My Ava:</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407375931i/10683674._SY540_.jpg" alt="good eyebrows dianna" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I discovered something new about KA that I love (the list just gets longer and longer). <div id="review_2093357872" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2093357872" />
    <a title="Mindy Lou&#39;s Book Review" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44132489-mindy-lou-s-book-review"><img alt="Mindy Lou&#39;s Book Review" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1465424458p2/44132489.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2093357872?book_show_action=true">Sep 19, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mindy Lou&#39;s Book Review" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mindy Lou&#39;s Book Review" href="/user/show/44132489-mindy-lou-s-book-review">Mindy Lou&#39;s Book Review</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/22518402-rock-chick-revenge">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44132489-mindy-lou-s-book-review?shelf=2018">2018</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2093357872" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9148469768639868713">If you've read previous Rock Chick books, then you know what you are getting into with this one. <br/><br/>I'm still loving the series but I gotta admit, listening to these books back to back is making me less and less tolerant of the heroine's constant resistance to these hunky men. I love a good man chase woman story and this definitely provides it. I just think the women resisting goes on too long. less is more. <br/><br/>I really wanted to like Ava but she argued with Luke constantly. It got old. Real fast. It </span>
  <span id="freeText9148469768639868713" style="display:none">If you've read previous Rock Chick books, then you know what you are getting into with this one. <br /><br />I'm still loving the series but I gotta admit, listening to these books back to back is making me less and less tolerant of the heroine's constant resistance to these hunky men. I love a good man chase woman story and this definitely provides it. I just think the women resisting goes on too long. less is more. <br /><br />I really wanted to like Ava but she argued with Luke constantly. It got old. Real fast. It goes to show how much I love this group of people that I still gave this 4 stars despite having to deal with her character. <br /><br />Luke's hitting on previous heroines in previous books came back to bite him in the butt. This is one case where I don't blame Ava at all for being upset when she found out. However, I loved Luke. I pretty much love all the men in this group and they are making this series very worth it. <br /><br />The side characters continue to be a constant source of entertainment. While the heroines are getting on my nerves with the constant resistance, once they move on to a side character in the next book, I'm loving them as well. <br /><br />I'm nervous for the next book. Mace has been one I've been looking forward too but he broke up with his heroine a year prior and I really hope it's for reasons that I can deal with. On to his book...</span>
  <a data-text-id="9148469768639868713" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_390797935" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/390797935" />
    <a title="Tina &quot;IRead2Escape&quot;" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3082213-tina-iread2escape"><img alt="Tina &quot;IRead2Escape&quot;" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1556205538p2/3082213.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/390797935?book_show_action=true">Aug 13, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tina &quot;IRead2Escape&quot;" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tina &quot;IRead2Escape&quot;" href="/user/show/3082213-tina-iread2escape">Tina &quot;IRead2Escape&quot;</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3082213-tina-iread2escape?shelf=2014-reading-challenge">2014-reading-challenge</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3082213-tina-iread2escape?shelf=part-of-a-series">part-of-a-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3082213-tina-iread2escape?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3082213-tina-iread2escape?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3082213-tina-iread2escape?shelf=audio">audio</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3082213-tina-iread2escape?shelf=romantic-suspense">romantic-suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3082213-tina-iread2escape?shelf=re-read">re-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3082213-tina-iread2escape?shelf=2015-reading-challenge">2015-reading-challenge</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3082213-tina-iread2escape?shelf=2016-reading-challenge">2016-reading-challenge</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3082213-tina-iread2escape?shelf=2018-reading-challenge">2018-reading-challenge</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer390797935" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11734346010536510990">That's it! Stop the presses (I've always wanted to say that) I have found my favorite Rock Chick book. Of course, this could change by the time I read the next one and I am sure I will declare my love in a similarly dramatic way, but Luke and Ava have my loyalty thus far. <br/><br/>Ava Barlow has sworn off men. I mean let's face it, if there is a lying, cheating, no good man in the vicinity she'll find him. Even her own father left and he was the one ally she had in her home. There is only one man that ha</span>
  <span id="freeText11734346010536510990" style="display:none">That's it! Stop the presses (I've always wanted to say that) I have found my favorite Rock Chick book. Of course, this could change by the time I read the next one and I am sure I will declare my love in a similarly dramatic way, but Luke and Ava have my loyalty thus far. <br /><br />Ava Barlow has sworn off men. I mean let's face it, if there is a lying, cheating, no good man in the vicinity she'll find him. Even her own father left and he was the one ally she had in her home. There is only one man that has ever been perfect in her eyes and she just doesn't fit with him. She's even lost 75 pounds and completely reinvented herself to feel worthy of him. However, in her mind this still isn't enough. Unfortunately, she has to face him and ask for his help. Her best friend is married to a cheating, slimeball and she needs to find proof.<br /><br />Luke Stark was the boy next door to Ava Barlow. He was the one person she could lean on and she was that one person for him. It never got any further than friendship because he left home and left her all alone with her judgmental mother and sisters. Now he is an esteemed member of the Savage hot bunch and can help her when no one else can. He always liked that Ava was different than the rest of the women in her life. She was witty and funny and sweet. He liked her no matter her weight. Now, he just has to convince her that there is no such thing as her being good enough for him. He loves and wants her for who she is.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"I'm not lettin' you go. I'm not lettin' you push me away and I'm not giving up. I'm gonna keep working until I piece together what your Dad and those assholes tore from you. I'm gonna keep at you until you let me in. I'm not gonna stop until you tell me you're mine, until it comes straight from your mouth, preferably when I'm deep inside you and you're lookin' at me like you look at me when I'm close to makin' you come."</i>
</b><br /><br />Rock Chick Revenge is the 5th book in the Rock Chick and series and it has it all. Luke Stark is one sexy, alpha male. His patience and undeniable love for Ava is impossible to resist. There were times when Ava got to me a bit, because she refused to believe she was worthy of Luke. I get body issues and I understood her insecurities, but I felt she held on to them a bit too long. About halfway through I totally got over it. She redeemed herself in every way. Read this book! You won't be disappointed.<br /><br />You can find this review at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://tinar1121.blogspot.com">http://tinar1121.blogspot.com</a> &amp; <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://riverinaromantics.blogspot.com">http://riverinaromantics.blogspot.com</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="11734346010536510990" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_255717444" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/255717444" />
    <a title="Searock" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6641663-searock"><img alt="Searock" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1396402019p2/6641663.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/255717444?book_show_action=true">Jan 03, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Searock" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Searock" href="/user/show/6641663-searock">Searock</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer255717444" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3822933777540485868">I really liked it. I can't believe how much I liked this fun, sexy, fluffy bit o' goodness.<br/><br/>All of my issues about this series are still in play here, but were more palatable to me in this 5th installment. Its a good book full of young, goofy language and jam-packed with characters, tons of unfolding action and a little angsty goodness to boot. With the peccadilloes not poking me in the eye so much, I was able to enjoy the heck outta this story. <br/><br/>I could pick apart some things that irritated me ab</span>
  <span id="freeText3822933777540485868" style="display:none">I really liked it. I can't believe how much I liked this fun, sexy, fluffy bit o' goodness.<br /><br />All of my issues about this series are still in play here, but were more palatable to me in this 5th installment. Its a good book full of young, goofy language and jam-packed with characters, tons of unfolding action and a little angsty goodness to boot. With the peccadilloes not poking me in the eye so much, I was able to enjoy the heck outta this story. <br /><br />I could pick apart some things that irritated me about the writing, but I knew about this series before going in, so not sure it would be appropriate to do that. It would be like having a wonderful meal and complaining about the spice in the sauce or the veggie chosen or the heat it was at when it got to your table, but I knew going in I was eating at the "Cinnamon Squash" outdoor cafe. Just saying.<br /><br />I also have a million and one things I found here that I love about KA's writing, but I will just leave it at: It was a delightful read. <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="3822933777540485868" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ibUQd9f4Dx1MJfjvAPp/Rl9mPIaVDIkMBGA/RuSbxsnrqSjApryGGyBm9mEED5yi99lWRCY2uoBoJW0+8MXhmQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('HGjgDuGEqLiGbPSMXxKZWshRk0z+KBaP+zE6UR+G8NN+dNi5kMAhvuov+gJb53q+YO75jk0SJQOXdGgpC9jXgw==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer4453361894194427799">Kristen Ashley was born in Gary, Indiana, USA. She nearly killed her mother and herself making it into the world, seeing as she had the umbilical cord wrapped around her neck (already attempting to accessorise and she hadn't taken her first breath!). <br/><br/>Kristen grew up in Brownsburg, Indiana but has lived in Denver, Colorado and the West Country of England. Thus she has been blessed to have friends a</span>
  <span id="freeText4453361894194427799" style="display:none">Kristen Ashley was born in Gary, Indiana, USA. She nearly killed her mother and herself making it into the world, seeing as she had the umbilical cord wrapped around her neck (already attempting to accessorise and she hadn't taken her first breath!). <br /><br />Kristen grew up in Brownsburg, Indiana but has lived in Denver, Colorado and the West Country of England. Thus she has been blessed to have friends and family around the globe. Her posse is loopy (to say the least) but loopy is good when you want to write.<br /><br />Kristen was raised in a house with a large and multi-generational family. They lived on a very small farm in a small town in the heartland and existed amongst the strains of Glenn Miller, The Everly Brothers, REO Speedwagon and Whitesnake (and the wardrobes that matched).<br /><br />Needless to say, growing up in a house full of music, clothes and love was a good way to grow up. <br /><br />And as she keeps growing up, it keeps getting better.</span>
